[2;36m                    [0m         +        [35m/[0m[35m/[0m Validate tesseract path to prevent command injection                     [2m               [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         +        actualTessPath = [1;35mvalidateTesseractPath[0m[1m([0mactualTessPath[1m)[0m;                     [2m               [0m

[2;36m                    [0m              [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m               [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                              [2m               [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         +        if [1m([0m![1;35mpath.matches[0m[1m([0m[32m"^[0m[32m[[0m[32ma-zA-Z0-9/_\\-.:,\\\\[0m[32m][0m[32m+$"[0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                          [2m               [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         +                                                                                    [2m               [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         +        return path;                                                                [2m               [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         +    [1m}[0m                                                                               [2m               [0m
